< review>
I was in the market and looking for a fully loaded 2013 or 2012 Chevy Avalanche LTZ. and I found a 2012 Chevy Avalanche at A&A Auto Sales.

I happen to come across A&A Auto Sales located in Fontana. I called them right away and talked to Ahmad. Ahmad mentioned that the car was still available.

I made an appointment to look at the truck on Sunday December 27, 2020 at 10am. I packed up the family and we were on our way.

As we approached the driveway of the dealership, Ahmad had the truck prepared and ready to go and parked at the entrance. it was a great welcoming onto the dealerships property.

We were greeted by a salesman, but I personally asked for Ahmad since we had already been communicated up to this point about the vehicle.

The family and I took the 2012 Chevy Avalanche out for a test drive and we feel  in love with it. It was love at first sight,  but I had to get to know it inside and out before I proposed to be in a newly committed relationship, LOL!

I thoroughly looked the truck over in detail. The exterior and interior was very solid. It had all the bells and whistles. Black on Black body paint and interior, just what I wanted.

I could go on and on!

As a consumer I was very impressed with their customer service and the pure humbleness of Ahmad. Ahmad and I got a chance to speak to each other for a while and it was determined, Ahmad is a good man and has a great heart and love for family.

The deal was solid and I appreciate the quality customer service!

Thank you again Ahmad and staff!!

I LOVE MY 2012 CHEVY AVALANCHE!!!!</review>

The color and year and price was perfect so I was very much interested with working with this dealership to purchase this truck. Since I would be heading to CA within the next few weeks to visit family, I figured let's try for the truck now. I dealt with a salesperson named Esmeralda. She gave me what I believe was her personal number and said that I could contact her regarding the truck. After being reassured that the dealership does do business with neighboring states, I was prompted to do the online application for the truck. We did the application and I let Esmeralda know through text that we completed and submitted the application. Esmeralda text back in a timely manner saying she would check the status and to give her a "sec." That sec lasted days. I had to continuously keep texting her about the status of our application and sometimes days between would go by until a response. I was given the same answer as all the other times, "sorry I got busy, give me a sec." I replied "okay" and waited to hear back from Esmeralda, but now a week has gone by without any sort of response or communication regarding the online application for the truck we were very much interested in. It would have been nice to be treated as a priority as we know all clients are treated with at an actual dealership. We were just as serious about purchasing this vehicle as any other person is who walks in a dealership looking for a vehicle and yet we were disregarded from the whole process. A phone call or text saying our application wasn't accepted or the truck was sold or whatever the reason was for not being contacted back would have been nice. My advice for anyone who is a neighboring state of CA and is trying to pursue a vehicle, don't go about it with this place through the phone or online. <userid>108866392833495062790<//userid>< Review>
Star Wars Launch Bay is an interactive walkthrough attraction at Disneyland Park at the Disneyland Resort, Disney's Hollywood Studios at Walt Disney World Resort, and Shanghai Disneyland Park. The attraction for Disneyland Resort and Disney's Hollywood Studios was announced at D23 Expo 2015 on August 15, 2015 at the Disney Parks Presentation along with Star Wars: Galaxy's Edge, the Season of the Force events at each park, and an updated scene for Star Tours‚ÄìThe Adventures Continue. The attraction opened at each park at the start of their respective Season of the Force events, which was November 16, 2015 for Disneyland and December 4, 2015 at Disney's Hollywood Studios. The Shanghai Version opened on June 16, 2016 and closed June 2019.<//Review>

Preview center for the upcoming Star Wars Land combined with a gift shop and a display of the art of Star Wars!  it's a nice Retreat from the midday heat of Anaheim. Plenty of bench spaces and fully wheelchair accessible. There is a full-scale representation of what the new Star Wars land will look like that you can check out. They have a video presentation that talks about how they came to the design they did. This one is somewhat hidden. Make sure you get a look at it because it's well worth walking through!  #LetsGuide #10SecondsOf #Video</text>

<review>If you are a Star Wars fan then this spot is a must visit on your Disneyland trip. There's a ton of memorabilia to see, from scaled down models of different vehicles,  to life size costumes of some of your favorite characters.
They have meet and greets with Chewbaca, Darth Vader,  and Kylo Ren. On our visit there was a small wait time depending on who you wanted to see. Chewie had the longest wait, cuz who wouldn't want to see that giant furball.
There was a small interactive gaming area where you could play some Star Wars themed games like lego Star Wars or the Star Wars Angry Birds.
It was cool seeing the full sized costumes. For an easy $3000 you could take home a nice Darth Vader outfit complete with helmet and all. I personally liked the storm troopers.
So if you get a chance,  swing by while you are in Tomorrowland.</review>< Time>

<Review>If you're trying to get a little glow without the sunburn, this is definitely the place for it. The staff is friendly, knowledgable and great at making you comfortable. You'll need to be completely nude for this, so it's important to trust the ladies who are helping you out!

Pro Tips:
- Exfoliate 1-2 days before so any dry skin is scrubbed off in advance
- Don't make any big plans for a few hours after this, because your skin will feel a bit strange and clammy until you can shower
- Don't get anywhere near water until the technician says you can! I tried to wash our dog (idiotic) and a few splashes got on my leg (like a fool) so I had some tiny streaks.
- Wear loose fitting clothes for after the session</Review>< GmapID>

I've written a review on Yelp as well.  I've never had a problem with going here.  The girls are always nice, sweet and cute.

My spray tans have lasted as long as two weeks!  I've never had a problem with blotchiness or discoloration.

I've been going here for over 3 years.<//text>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
Just had lunch from here with my wife, the sandwiches were both delicious, I had the pulled pork sandwich and the peppers were an interesting and satisfying combination. The Jive Turkey sandwich though, which my wife shared a bite of, was exceptional. A wonderfully stacked sandwich that had an excellent combination of flavors.

We also had the orzo and thai peanut deli salads, my wife enjoyed her orzo but I did not enjoy the thai salad. The dressing didn't capture either peanut sauce or the typical thai cucumber salad dressing I was expecting. I was disappointed but we both enjoyed our sandwiches so much that they've still earned five stars for speed, flavor and value.

We will definitely be back to try more offerings from this little gem.</Text>

<Date>1202871518519</Date><Rating>1< /Rating><Text>Pros
Choose this unless you buy insurance and you mind bad car.

Cons
Bundles of hidden costs and no transparent business

Full Review
1. Rental fee itself is relatively cheap. This is the major reason I chose this company online.

2. Rental auto was the worst I ever rented.

3. Buying full coverage insurance cost $39/day for a full size car. No mention about this cost online.

4. They charge, without informing you, $4.99 for road services (which is an option) to be rendered when thrifty's own rental car fails on the road. No apologizing for not informing me of the inclusion of the fee. Staff acted as if I must be a weird guy not to choose the option.
-- Renting cars in poor condition, and then we pay for the service invoked by the poor condition of the car!!!

5. They change many options I had chosen online (even the car size (dollar rent-a-car, same ownership as thrifty I think) without saying anything. Having unexpected such unsual (usual for them?) behavior, I signed the contract.

6. Overall, you pay the same or more for a worse car and unpleasant service if you choose thrifty than if you choose other well-known rent-a-car company.

<text>Lesson learned, the name says it all! Thrifty and cheapest option? Yes. Quality and good customer service? Absolutely not!

Not only did we get the runaround from the poor signage at the airport (we needed to "check-in" before we picked up our keys on a different floor) but we encountered the horror that so many other reviewers mentioned of unimaginably SLOW lines with 2.5 associates scrambling (yes one of them disappeared 1/2 through the shift). I was worried we'd miss the pick up time of 11:15am since half an hour passed and we only moved a few feet forward. Then I realized time was not a concept in this vortex. Somewhat fortunately for us we were not at the worst part of it since more disgruntled bodies soon piled in from other flights arriving later.

I did what any reasonable consumer would do to pass the time. I indulged myself on the horrible Yelp reviews from other poor souls, and pitied myself for not seeing the warning signs earlier.  By noon we were nearly at the front of the line seeing the light at the end of this interminable tunnel. We were finally next!!! Surprisingly the actual interactions with the associate were pleasant and I felt bad that one of her co-workers left her hanging as she was supposed to take her lunch break right now.
